[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"VM Periodic Task Thread"[0m[39m [0m[33mos_prio[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[33mcpu[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m47[0m[1;36m.[0m[39m26ms [0m[33melapsed[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m27[0m[1;36m.[0m[39m90s [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mtid[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0x000055d8e6dfbee0[0m[39m [0m[33mnid[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0x21[0m[39m waiting on condition  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNI global refs: [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m, weak refs: [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run against `CompressTarFuzzer` timed out after approximately [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds. The thread dump shows the `main` thread stuck in Java’s big-integer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdivision logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and related methods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invoked by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.divide` calls within Apache Commons Compress’s TAR PAX header [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing of TAR archive handling, the fuzzer’s `fuzzerTestOneInput` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry point in `CompressTarFuzzer` triggered a long-running or effectively infinite[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop in the BigDecimal division routines. As a result, libFuzzer terminated the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution due to a timeout.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a performance hang [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtimeout[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than a memory corruption or [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception. No explicit security vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., crash or data leak[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobserved; instead, malformed or specially crafted PAX header values cause excessive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The `main` thread is in state RUNNABLE, consuming CPU in [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The division logic is invoked by `BigDecimal.divide` and related methods in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • These BigDecimal operations are called by [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` while processing PAX headers [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`processPaxHeader`, `updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Control passes through `TarFile.getNextTarEntry` and constructors, ultimately [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked by the fuzz harness.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads appear blocked or involved in the hang; the issue is confined [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto numerical processing.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds**  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Review parsing of decimal-seconds values to identify inputs that drive [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigDecimal division into worst-case performance.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **BigDecimal.divide calls in Apache Commons Compress**  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Examine scale/precision handling and zero-stripping logic that may trigger [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpensive division algorithms.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **PAX header processing flow**  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Trace how PAX header key-value pairs are handled [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`processPaxHeader`, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateEntryFromPaxHeaders`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and how invalid or large numeric strings propagate [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto BigDecimal.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzz harness entry point**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Although not the root cause, confirm how [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` supplies data to `TarFile` and whether it [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexercises timeout-sensitive code paths.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis investigation scope should provide a holistic view of why certain inputs cause[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprolonged BigDecimal operations and eventual fuzzer timeouts.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m: * An entry in a <a [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"https[0m[32m://www.gnu.org/software/tar/manual/html_node/Standard.html"[0m[39m>Tar [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m: * It consists of the entry's header, as well as the entry's File. Entries can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe instantiated in one of three[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m: * ways, depending on how they are to be used.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m: * TarEntries that are created from the header bytes read from an archive are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstantiated with the [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m constructor.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m: * These entries will be used when extracting from or listing the contents of an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive. These entries have their header filled in using the header bytes. They[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m: * also set the File to null, since they reference an archive entry not a file.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m: * TarEntries that are created from Files that are to be written into an archive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare instantiated with the [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m or[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m: * [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link TarArchiveEntry#[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m constructor. These entries have[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir header filled in using the File's information. They also keep a reference[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m: * to the File for convenience when writing entries.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m: * Finally, TarEntries can be constructed from nothing but a name. This allows [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe programmer to construct the entry by hand, for instance when only an[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m: * InputStream is available for writing to the archive, and the header [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minformation is constructed from other information. In this case the header fields [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare set[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m: * to defaults and the File is set to null.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m: * The C structure for a Tar Entry's header is:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m: * <pre>[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m: * struct header [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m: *   char name[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.NAMELEN    - offset   [0m[1;36m0[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m: *   char mode[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.MODELEN    - offset [0m[1;36m100[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m: *   char uid[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.UIDLEN     - offset [0m[1;36m108[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m: *   char gid[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.GIDLEN     - offset [0m[1;36m116[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m: *   char size[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.SIZELEN    - offset [0m[1;36m124[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m: *   char mtime[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.MODTIMELEN - offset [0m[1;36m136[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m: *   char chksum[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.CHKSUMLEN  - offset [0m[1;36m148[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m: *   char linkflag[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m                         - offset [0m[1;36m156[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m: *   char linkname[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.NAMELEN    - offset [0m[1;36m157[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m: *   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m The following fields are only present in new-style POSIX tar archives:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m: *   char magic[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.MAGICLEN   - offset [0m[1;36m257[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m: *   char version[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.VERSIONLEN - offset [0m[1;36m263[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m94[0m[39m: *   char uname[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.UNAMELEN   - offset [0m[1;36m265[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m95[0m[39m: *   char gname[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.GNAMELEN   - offset [0m[1;36m297[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m: *   char devmajor[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.DEVLEN     - offset [0m[1;36m329[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m97[0m[39m: *   char devminor[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m TarConstants.DEVLEN     - offset [0m[1;36m337[0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m: *   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Used if [0m[32m"name"[0m[39m field is not long enough to hold the path[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m: *   char pad[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m NULs                    - offset [0m[1;36m500[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m: * [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m header;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m: * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m: * All unused bytes are set to null. New-style GNU tar files are slightly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferent from the above. For values of size larger than 077777777777L [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m11[0m[39m 7s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The performance hang arises in `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`, where [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaliciously long fractional parts [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. thousands of digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m cause [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mmovePointRight[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to perform [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworst-case big-integer division.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing regex `-?\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allows unbounded fractional digits [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`\d*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, permitting attacker-controlled input to drive BigDecimal into expensive [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation loops.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Validate the PAX header time string before parsing.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Preserve support for negative timestamps, up to [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m integral digits.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Preserve sub-second precision up to nanoseconds [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d. Throw `IOException` on invalid formats or out-of-range values.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoid modifying or extending fuzz harness, utility functions, or tests.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Tighten the regular expression to cap the fractional part at [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits:  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change the pattern from  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Rationale: Enforces at most [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal places [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisallows trailing dot without digits.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Update the accompanying Javadoc comment to reflect the new maximum precision [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“up to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the parsing logic in `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` unchanged; [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid inputs with too many fractional digits will now fail regex validation and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow `IOException`, preventing any `BigDecimal` calls on untrusted long strings.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `TarArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the static pattern definition at lines [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m:  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace with:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m**  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         * Regex for validating PAX extended header time fields:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *  - integral part: optional [0m[32m'-'[0m[39m plus [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfits in long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *  - optional fractional part: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m plus [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond precision[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         *[0m[35m/[0m[39m  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Update the Javadoc above to note “maximum [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits” instead of an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munbounded fraction.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun all unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding TAR PAX header tests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno regressions.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Re-run the `CompressTarFuzzer`; confirm that inputs with excessive decimal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits now trigger a quick `IOException` rather than a hang.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side Effects  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Restricting fractional digits directly thwarts the source of exponential CPU [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwork while maintaining full nanosecond accuracy.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rejecting values with >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fraction digits is consistent with POSIX/PAX [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing valid archives [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith ≤[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unaffected; tests [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould pass unchanged.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side effect: very high-precision timestamps [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtreated as invalid and result in `IOException`. Given the PAX spec, this is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macceptable.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Code  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other archive formats [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., ZIP extra-field timestamps[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in Apache Commons [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moften cap fractional precision to prevent BigDecimal misuse.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change aligns `TarArchiveEntry` with best practices in `ParsingUtils` and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TimeUtils`, which validate and bound numeric inputs before high-cost parsing.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
